\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00095}00095 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00096}00096 \textcolor{comment}{** Compilers are starting to complain about the use of sprintf() and strcpy(),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00097}00097 \textcolor{comment}{** saying they are unsafe.  So we define our own versions of those routines too.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00098}00098 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00099}00099 \textcolor{comment}{** There are three routines here:  lemon\_sprintf(), lemon\_vsprintf(), and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00100}00100 \textcolor{comment}{** lemon\_addtext(). The first two are replacements for sprintf() and vsprintf().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00101}00101 \textcolor{comment}{** The third is a helper routine for vsnprintf() that adds texts to the end of a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00102}00102 \textcolor{comment}{** buffer, making sure the buffer is always zero-\/terminated.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00103}00103 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00104}00104 \textcolor{comment}{** The string formatter is a minimal subset of stdlib sprintf() supporting only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00105}00105 \textcolor{comment}{** a few simply conversions:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00106}00106 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00107}00107 \textcolor{comment}{**   \%d}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00108}00108 \textcolor{comment}{**   \%s}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00109}00109 \textcolor{comment}{**   \%.*s}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00110}00110 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00111}00111 \textcolor{comment}{*/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00594}00594 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00595}00595 \textcolor{comment}{** This module implements routines use to construct the yy\_action[] table.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00596}00596 \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00597}00597 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00598}00598 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00599}00599 \textcolor{comment}{** The state of the yy\_action table under construction is an instance of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00600}00600 \textcolor{comment}{** the following structure.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00601}00601 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00602}00602 \textcolor{comment}{** The yy\_action table maps the pair (state\_number, lookahead) into an}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00603}00603 \textcolor{comment}{** action\_number.  The table is an array of integers pairs.  The state\_number}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00604}00604 \textcolor{comment}{** determines an initial offset into the yy\_action array.  The lookahead}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00605}00605 \textcolor{comment}{** value is then added to this initial offset to get an index X into the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00606}00606 \textcolor{comment}{** yy\_action array. If the aAction[X].lookahead equals the value of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00607}00607 \textcolor{comment}{** of the lookahead input, then the value of the action\_number output is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00608}00608 \textcolor{comment}{** aAction[X].action.  If the lookaheads do not match then the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00609}00609 \textcolor{comment}{** default action for the state\_number is returned.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00610}00610 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00611}00611 \textcolor{comment}{** All actions associated with a single state\_number are first entered}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00612}00612 \textcolor{comment}{** into aLookahead[] using multiple calls to acttab\_action().  Then the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00613}00613 \textcolor{comment}{** actions for that single state\_number are placed into the aAction[]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00614}00614 \textcolor{comment}{** array with a single call to acttab\_insert().  The acttab\_insert() call}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00615}00615 \textcolor{comment}{** also resets the aLookahead[] array in preparation for the next}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00616}00616 \textcolor{comment}{** state number.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00617}00617 \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00618}\mbox{\hyperlink{structlookahead__action}{00618}} \textcolor{keyword}{struct }\mbox{\hyperlink{structlookahead__action}{lookahead\_action}} \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00698}00698 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00699}00699 \textcolor{comment}{** Add the transaction set built up with prior calls to acttab\_action()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00700}00700 \textcolor{comment}{** into the current action table.  Then reset the transaction set back}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00701}00701 \textcolor{comment}{** to an empty set in preparation for a new round of acttab\_action() calls.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00702}00702 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00703}00703 \textcolor{comment}{** Return the offset into the action table of the new transaction.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00704}00704 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00705}00705 \textcolor{comment}{** If the makeItSafe parameter is true, then the offset is chosen so that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00706}00706 \textcolor{comment}{** it is impossible to overread the yy\_lookaside[] table regardless of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00707}00707 \textcolor{comment}{** the lookaside token.  This is done for the terminal symbols, as they}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00708}00708 \textcolor{comment}{** come from external inputs and can contain syntax errors.  When makeItSafe}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00709}00709 \textcolor{comment}{** is false, there is more flexibility in selecting offsets, resulting in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00710}00710 \textcolor{comment}{** a smaller table.  For non-\/terminal symbols, which are never syntax errors,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00711}00711 \textcolor{comment}{** makeItSafe can be false.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00712}00712 \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l00713}\mbox{\hyperlink{musami_8c_09_09_ad44309f3ae83c1fda003d7ac70643241}{00713}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} \mbox{\hyperlink{musami_8c_09_09_ad44309f3ae83c1fda003d7ac70643241}{acttab\_insert}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{structacttab}{acttab}} *p, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} makeItSafe)\{}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01259}01259 \textcolor{comment}{/* Resolve a conflict between the two given actions.  If the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01260}01260 \textcolor{comment}{** conflict can't be resolved, return non-\/zero.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01261}01261 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01262}01262 \textcolor{comment}{** NO LONGER TRUE:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01263}01263 \textcolor{comment}{**   To resolve a conflict, first look to see if either action}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01264}01264 \textcolor{comment}{**   is on an error rule.  In that case, take the action which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01265}01265 \textcolor{comment}{**   is not associated with the error rule.  If neither or both}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01266}01266 \textcolor{comment}{**   actions are associated with an error rule, then try to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01267}01267 \textcolor{comment}{**   use precedence to resolve the conflict.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01268}01268 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01269}01269 \textcolor{comment}{** If either action is a SHIFT, then it must be apx.  This}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01270}01270 \textcolor{comment}{** function won't work if apx-\/>type==REDUCE and apy-\/>type==SHIFT.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01271}01271 \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01272}01272 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} resolve\_conflict(}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01273}01273   \textcolor{keyword}{struct} \mbox{\hyperlink{structaction}{action}} *apx,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01274}01274   \textcolor{keyword}{struct} \mbox{\hyperlink{structaction}{action}} *apy}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01275}01275 )\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01276}01276   \textcolor{keyword}{struct }\mbox{\hyperlink{structsymbol}{symbol}} *spx, *spy;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01277}01277   \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} errcnt = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01278}01278   assert( apx-\/>\mbox{\hyperlink{structaction_a8bb419de6aa7116057d284c32003e623}{sp}}==apy-\/>\mbox{\hyperlink{structaction_a8bb419de6aa7116057d284c32003e623}{sp}} );  \textcolor{comment}{/* Otherwise there would be no conflict */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01279}01279   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}( apx-\/>\mbox{\hyperlink{structaction_ac0dce56259e3c49ee6a14e738ac63f0d}{type}}==\mbox{\hyperlink{musami_8c_09_09_a9695563ba2c3d4e59f4680439da60d8ba1ce4ab037343ee04fbf20ceb2ebc5081}{SHIFT}} \&\& apy-\/>\mbox{\hyperlink{structaction_ac0dce56259e3c49ee6a14e738ac63f0d}{type}}==\mbox{\hyperlink{musami_8c_09_09_a9695563ba2c3d4e59f4680439da60d8ba1ce4ab037343ee04fbf20ceb2ebc5081}{SHIFT}} )\{}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01748}01748   \textcolor{comment}{/* Assign sequential rule numbers.  Start with 0.  Put rules that have no}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01749}01749 \textcolor{comment}{  ** reduce action C-\/code associated with them last, so that the switch()}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01836}01836 \textcolor{comment}{** Let "{}ptr"{} be a pointer to some structure which is at the head of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01837}01837 \textcolor{comment}{** a null-\/terminated list.  Then to sort the list call:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01838}01838 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01839}01839 \textcolor{comment}{**     ptr = msort(ptr,\&(ptr-\/>next),cmpfnc);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01840}01840 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01841}01841 \textcolor{comment}{** In the above, "{}cmpfnc"{} is a pointer to a function which compares}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01842}01842 \textcolor{comment}{** two instances of the structure and returns an integer, as in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01843}01843 \textcolor{comment}{** strcmp.  The second argument is a pointer to the pointer to the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01844}01844 \textcolor{comment}{** second element of the linked list.  This address is used to compute}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01845}01845 \textcolor{comment}{** the offset to the "{}next"{} field within the structure.  The offset to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01846}01846 \textcolor{comment}{** the "{}next"{} field must be constant for all structures in the list.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01847}01847 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l01848}01848 \textcolor{comment}{** The function returns a new pointer which is the head of the list}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l05552}05552 \textcolor{comment}{** (non-\/terminals).  And MULTITERMINAL symbols (created using the}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{musami_8c_09_09_source_l05558}05558 \textcolor{comment}{** smallest parser tables in SQLite.}}
